    23	## Coverage Theater Prevention
    24	
    25	- Passing tests that only assert `ok: true` without validating envelope shape.
    26	- Testing fallback code by asserting output exists, but not asserting downgrade indicators.
    27	- Source-inspection tests that never run (`run=False`, disabled guards left in place forever).
    28	- Tests that verify only one forecast endpoint while claiming horizon consistency for three endpoints.
    29	- Mock-only ingest tests that never verify shared table contract fields (`run_id`, status vocabulary).
    30	- Gate scripts that check legacy route shapes (`/api/cron`) instead of architecture policy.
    31	- Freshness tests that verify one date field but ignore mixed-vintage semantics.
    32	
    33	## Fitness-to-Purpose Scenarios
    34	
    35	### Scenario 1: Ingest Telemetry Contract Split
    36	
    37	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-001]
    38	
    39	**What happened:** `ops.ingest_run` requires `run_id`, but legacy SQL writers insert rows without it while TS helpers write uppercase status enums. This permits partial observability and fragmented status semantics across the same table.
    40	
    41	**The requirement:** All ingest writers must use one lifecycle contract: explicit `run_id`, canonical status vocabulary, and deterministic start/success/failure transitions.
    42	
    43	**How to verify:** `test_req001_all_ingest_writers_include_run_id_and_canonical_status` in `quality/test_functional.py`.
    44	
    45	### Scenario 2: Forbidden Cron Surface Drift
    46	
    47	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-002]
    48	
    49	**What happened:** Architecture policy forbids Vercel cron routes, but middleware and verification logic still encode `/api/cron` assumptions. This can block compliant builds or push engineers toward forbidden route resurrection.
    50	
    51	**The requirement:** Auth middleware and verification gates must validate pg_cron-only architecture without requiring `/api/cron` endpoints.
    52	
    53	**How to verify:** `test_req002_no_runtime_or_gate_dependency_on_api_cron_path` in `quality/test_functional.py`.
    54	
    55	### Scenario 3: Intraday Fallback Promise Divergence
    56	
    57	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-003]
    58	
    59	**What happened:** `/api/zl/intraday` claims a 15m→1m fallback in comments while querying only `mkt.price_15m`. Consumers can trust resilience that is not implemented.
    60	
    61	**The requirement:** Either implement fallback behavior to `mkt.price_1m` or remove fallback claims and align client assumptions.
    62	
    63	**How to verify:** `test_req003_intraday_route_contract_matches_implemented_fallback` in `quality/test_functional.py`.
    64	
    65	### Scenario 4: Envelope Contract Drift Across Surfaces
    66	
    67	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-004]
    68	
    69	**What happened:** Route responses, shared API contract types, and parity gate checks disagree about optional vs required envelope fields (`warning`, shape differences). False-negative parity failures can mask real regressions.
    70	
    71	**The requirement:** Contract types, route envelopes, and verification scripts must share one consistent envelope policy.
    72	
    73	**How to verify:** `test_req004_contract_and_gate_align_on_warning_semantics` in `quality/test_functional.py`.
    74	
    75	### Scenario 5: Mixed-Vintage Freshness Misread
    76	
    77	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-005]
    78	
    79	**What happened:** Risk-factor API sets canonical `as_of_date` to oldest component date while also exposing min/max range. Dashboard messaging can be interpreted as fully stale even when only part of vector is stale.
    80	
    81	**The requirement:** Mixed-vintage data must be explicitly signaled as degraded with field-level transparency.
    82	
    83	**How to verify:** `test_req005_risk_factor_payload_exposes_mixed_vintage_metadata` in `quality/test_functional.py`.
    84	
    85	### Scenario 6: Forecast Horizon Normalization Drift
    86	
    87	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-006]
    88	
    89	**What happened:** `normalizeHorizon` logic is duplicated across three endpoints. A one-file edit can desynchronize forecast, target-zone, and probability surfaces.
    90	
    91	**The requirement:** Horizon normalization constants and mapping behavior must remain equivalent across all forecast-facing endpoints.
    92	
    93	**How to verify:** `test_req006_normalize_horizon_logic_is_identical_across_three_routes` in `quality/test_functional.py`.
    94	
    95	### Scenario 7: Snapshot Source Whitelist Regression
    96	
    97	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-004]
    98	
    99	**What happened:** Snapshot source labels are hard-whitelisted. A source-label drift can silently null out snapshots and trigger unannounced fallback narratives.
   100	
   101	**The requirement:** Whitelist changes must be deliberate, and fallback behavior must expose reliability downgrade cues.
   102	
   103	**How to verify:** `test_scenario_snapshot_source_whitelist_is_explicit_and_auditable` in `quality/test_functional.py`.
   104	
   105	### Scenario 8: Scaffold Pipeline Misreported as Ready
   106	
   107	**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-001]
   108	
   109	**What happened:** `pipeline.py --all` includes scaffold phases returning `status: scaffold`. Operators can read full-run completion as inference readiness.
   110	
   111	**The requirement:** Scaffold status must remain explicit and blocked from “ready” interpretation until implemented.
   112	
   113	**How to verify:** `test_scenario_pipeline_order_and_scaffold_modules_are_visible` in `quality/test_functional.py`.

from __future__ import annotations

import re
import unittest
from pathlib import Path


REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[1]


def read_text(rel_path: str) -> str:
    return (REPO_ROOT / rel_path).read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")


class SpecRequirementsFunctionalTest(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_req001_all_ingest_writers_include_run_id_and_canonical_status(self) -> None:
        """[Req: inferred — REQ-001] All ingest writers use unified run-id lifecycle contract."""
        ddl = read_text("supabase/migrations/202603180009_ops_vegas.sql")
        legacy_ingest = read_text("supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql")
        trusted_ingest = read_text("supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql")
        ts_writer = read_text("lib/server/ingest-run.ts")

        self.assertRegex(ddl, r"run_id\s+UUID\s+PRIMARY\s+KEY")
        self.assertIn("run_id", trusted_ingest)
        self.assertIn("run_id", ts_writer)
        # Desired-state assertion: legacy SQL writer should also include run_id inserts.
        self.assertRegex(legacy_ingest, r"INSERT INTO ops\.ingest_run \(run_id,")

    def test_req002_no_runtime_or_gate_dependency_on_api_cron_path(self) -> None:
        """[Req: inferred — REQ-002] Cron route shape is not required by middleware or verification gates."""
        proxy = read_text("lib/supabase/proxy.ts")
        gate3 = read_text("scripts/verify/gate3.sh")
        agents = read_text("AGENTS.md")

        self.assertIn("No Inngest. No Vercel Cron.", agents)
        self.assertNotIn("/api/cron/", proxy)
        self.assertNotRegex(gate3, r"rg\s+app/api/cron")

    def test_req003_intraday_route_contract_matches_implemented_fallback(self) -> None:
        """[Req: inferred — REQ-003] Intraday fallback comments match executable query behavior."""
        route = read_text("app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts")
        self.assertIn("fallback", route.lower())
        self.assertIn("mkt.price_15m", route)
        # Desired-state assertion: explicit query path to 1m source exists when fallback is documented.
        self.assertIn("mkt.price_1m", route)

    def test_req004_contract_and_gate_align_on_warning_semantics(self) -> None:
        """[Req: inferred — REQ-004] Optional warning semantics are consistent across contract and parity gates."""
        api_contract = read_text("lib/contracts/api.ts")
        gate6 = read_text("scripts/verify/gate6.sh")

        self.assertRegex(api_contract, r"warning\?:\s*string")
        # Desired-state assertion: gate should not require warning on every success payload.
        self.assertNotRegex(gate6, r'\.warning\s*\|\|\s*empty')

    def test_req005_risk_factor_payload_exposes_mixed_vintage_metadata(self) -> None:
        """[Req: inferred — REQ-005] Mixed-vintage freshness metadata is emitted and rendered."""
        api = read_text("app/api/dashboard/risk-factors/route.ts")
        ui = read_text("components/dashboard/MarketRiskFactors.tsx")

        for field in ["as_of_date", "as_of_date_min", "as_of_date_max", "mixed_vintage"]:
            self.assertIn(field, api)
        self.assertRegex(ui, r"mixed[-_ ]vintage|as_of_date_min|as_of_date_max")

    68

    70

    74	- REQ-003 vs REQ-005: degradation/fallback communication consistency.

    57	## Running the Audit
    58	
    59	1. Execute prompt against three models independently.
    60	2. Save raw outputs:
    61	   - `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-auditor1.md`
    62	   - `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-auditor2.md`
    63	   - `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-auditor3.md`
    64	3. Produce triage:
    65	   - `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-triage.md`
    66	
    67	## Council Status Block (mandatory)
    68	
    69	Triage must start with:
    70	
    71	```markdown
    72	## Council Status
    73	- Auditor 1: Fresh report received (YYYY-MM-DD)
    74	- Auditor 2: Fresh report received (YYYY-MM-DD)
    75	- Auditor 3: Fresh report received (YYYY-MM-DD)
    76	```
    77	
    78	If fewer than 3 reports are usable, explicitly log effective council size.
    79	
    80	## Confidence and Triage Rules
    81	
    82	| Confidence | Found By | Action |
    83	|---|---|---|
    84	| Highest | 3/3 | Confirm unless verification probe disproves |
    85	| High | 2/3 | Confirm with targeted verification |
    86	| Needs verification | 1/3 | Run verification probe before classification |
    87	
    88	## Verification Probes Must Be Executable
    89	
    90	For disputed findings, create executable assertions in one of:
    91	
    92	- `quality/mechanical/verify.sh`, or
    93	- `quality/spec_audits/triage_probes.sh`
    94	
    95	Requirements:
    96	- Rejections require passing assertions proving claim false.
    97	- Confirmations require failing assertions proving claim true.
    98	- Every assertion cites exact evidence line.
    99	
   100	## Categorize Confirmed Findings
   101	
   102	Use one of:
   103	- Spec bug
   104	- Design decision
   105	- Real code bug
   106	- Documentation gap
   107	- Missing test
   108	- Inferred requirement wrong
   109	
   110	## Cross-Artifact Consistency
   111	
   112	Compare triage against Phase 3 code review findings.
   113	If conflict exists on same factual claim, run verification probe and record resolution.
   114	
   115	## Fix Execution Rules
   116	
   117	- Group fixes by subsystem.
   118	- Avoid mega-prompts.
   119	- Require regression tests for real code bugs.
   120	
   121	## Output Artifacts
   122	
   123	- `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-auditor*.md`
   124	- `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-triage.md`
   125	- `quality/spec_audits/triage_probes.sh` (if probes used)

     1	# TDD Verification Protocol: ZINC-FUSION-V16
     2	> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.6 — Andrew Stellman
     3	> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16
     4	
     5	## Scope
     6	
     7	Run red/green verification for every confirmed bug in `quality/BUGS.md`.
     8	
     9	## Spec-grounded test requirements
    10	
    11	For each BUG-NNN:
    12	
    13	1. Read associated requirement (`REQ-NNN`) from `quality/REQUIREMENTS.md`.
    14	2. Read bug `spec basis` field.
    15	3. Build assertions using spec language (not internal-only shorthand).
    16	4. Add traceability comment with requirement ID, bug ID, and spec passage.
    17	
    18	## Red-Green Execution
    19	
    20	For each bug with regression and fix patches:
    21	
    22	1. **Red phase:** run regression test on unpatched code. Expected: fail.
    23	2. **Green phase:** apply fix patch and rerun same test. Expected: pass.
    24	3. **Record:** write logs and update closure status.
    25	
    26	If no fix patch exists:
    27	- Red phase still required.
    28	- Green phase marked `skipped`.
    29	- Verdict is `confirmed open`.
    30	
    31	## Framework adaptation
    32	
    33	Project baseline test framework: Python `unittest`.
    34	
    35	Primary command pattern:
    36	
    37	```bash
    38	python -m unittest quality.test_regression
    39	```
    40	
    41	For per-bug runs:
    42	
    43	```bash
    44	python -m unittest quality.test_regression.TestRegression.test_bug_nnn
    45	```
    46	
    47	## Required Log Artifacts
    48	
    49	For each confirmed BUG-NNN:
    50	
    51	- `quality/results/BUG-NNN.red.log`
    52	- `quality/results/BUG-NNN.green.log` (if fix patch exists)
    53	
    54	First line must be one of: `RED`, `GREEN`, `NOT_RUN`, `ERROR`.
    55	
    56	## Log Template
    57	
    58	```text
    59	RED
    60	--- Test output for BUG-NNN red phase ---
    61	Command: python -m unittest quality.test_regression.TestRegression.test_bug_nnn
    62	Exit code: 1
    63	[stdout/stderr]
    64	```
    65

    67

    70	```json
    71	{

    81	      "green_phase": "pass",
    82	      "verdict": "TDD verified",
    83	      "regression_patch": "quality/patches/BUG-001-regression-test.patch",
    84	      "fix_patch": "quality/patches/BUG-001-fix.patch",
    85	      "fix_patch_present": true,
    86	      "patch_gate_passed": true,
    87	      "writeup_path": "quality/writeups/BUG-001.md",
    88	      "junit_red": "tdd-red-BUG-001.xml",
    89	      "junit_green": "tdd-green-BUG-001.xml",
    90	      "junit_available": false,
    91	      "notes": ""
    92	    }
    93	  ],
    94	  "summary": {
    95	    "total": 1,
    96	    "verified": 1,
    97	    "confirmed_open": 0,
    98	    "red_failed": 0,

   100	  }
   101	}
   102	```
   103	
   104	Allowed verdicts:
   105	- `TDD verified`
   106	- `red failed`
   107	- `green failed`
   108	- `confirmed open`
   109	- `deferred`
   110	
   111	## Traceability Output
   112	
   113	Generate `quality/TDD_TRACEABILITY.md`:
   114	
   115	| Bug ID | Requirement ID | Spec Doc | Spec Section | Behavioral Contract | Test File:Function | Red Result | Green Result |
   116	|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
   117	
   118	Every confirmed bug must have a row.
   119	
   120	## Patch Gate
   121	
   122	Before bug closure:
   123	
   124	1. `git apply --check quality/patches/BUG-NNN-regression-test.patch`
   125	2. `git apply --check quality/patches/BUG-NNN-fix.patch` (if present)
   126	3. Run syntax/compile check after applying patches in temporary worktree.
   127	
   128	If patch gate fails, repair patch before claiming closure.
   129	
   130	## Execution UX
   131	
   132	### Phase 1: Plan
   133	
   134	Show bug verification queue as numbered table.
   135	
   136	### Phase 2: Progress
   137	
   138	One-line progress per bug:
   139	- `FAIL ✓ -> PASS ✓`
   140	- `FAIL ✓ -> SKIPPED (no fix patch)`
   141	- `ERROR (environment)`
   142	
   143	### Phase 3: Results
   144	
   145	Report totals:
   146	- Verified
   147	- Confirmed open
   148	- Red failed
   149	- Green failed
   150	- Deferred
   151	
   152	## Upstream-ready report block
   153	
   154	For each `TDD verified` bug include:
   155	
   156	1. One-sentence spec violation summary.
   157	2. FAIL→PASS terminal output snippet.
   158	3. Regression test path.
   159	4. Fix patch path.

    33	## Pass 2: Requirement Verification
    34	
    35	#### REQ-001: `ops.ingest_run` writers MUST use one normalized run contract
    36	**Status**: VIOLATED
    37	**Evidence**: `supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql:50-52,90-92,138-140,218-220`; `lib/server/ingest-run.ts:3,17,38,58`; `supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql:56,365,382`
    38	**Analysis**: SQL intraday/rollup writers omit `run_id` and use mixed status vocabulary with other writers.
    39	**Severity**: High (observability drift + lifecycle fragmentation risk).

    41	#### REQ-002: Verification/auth scaffolding MUST not require `/api/cron`
    42	**Status**: VIOLATED
    43	**Evidence**: `lib/supabase/proxy.ts:15-17,39-42`; `scripts/verify/gate3.sh:5`; `AGENTS.md:44-45`
    44	**Analysis**: middleware and Gate 3 both encode forbidden `/api/cron` assumptions.
    45	**Severity**: High (policy drift can block compliant builds and weaken auth boundaries).

    49	**Evidence**: `app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts:10-16`
    50	**Analysis**: fallback text claims 1m fallback; implementation has only 15m query path.

    52

    54	**Status**: VIOLATED

    56	**Analysis**: optional field semantics and envelope family coverage are inconsistent across contract/gate/endpoint.

    68	**Analysis**: constants and legacy map parity are intact, but unknown-horizon drop behavior is silent and unlogged in all three sites.

    74	**Requirements**: REQ-001, REQ-004
    75	**What REQ-001 claims**: one canonical ingest lifecycle/status contract.
    76	**What REQ-004 claims**: one canonical envelope required/optional contract.

    79	**Analysis**: both contract families drift in opposite directions (writer split + gate over-constraint), indicating normalization principles are not uniformly applied.
    80	**Impact**: false telemetry semantics and false parity failures.

    83	**Requirements**: REQ-002, REQ-004

    86	**Consistency**: INCONSISTENT
    87	**Code evidence**: `scripts/verify/gate3.sh:5`; `lib/supabase/proxy.ts:15-17`; `scripts/verify/gate6.sh:74-80`
    88	**Analysis**: gate surfaces encode stale assumptions that no longer match architecture and contract authority.
    89	**Impact**: release gates can fail for policy-compliant builds.

    91	#### Shared Concept: Forecast surface consistency (shape + horizon behavior)
    92	**Requirements**: REQ-004, REQ-006
    93	**What REQ-004 claims**: envelope family consistency and documented exceptions.
    94	**What REQ-006 claims**: equivalent horizon normalization across all forecast-facing endpoints.
    95	**Consistency**: INCONSISTENT
    96	**Code evidence**: `app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts:54-57,61-64,97-100`; `app/api/zl/forecast/route.ts:61-63`; `app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts:61-63`; `scripts/verify/gate6.sh:69-181`
    97	**Analysis**: forecast-targets shape is ungoverned by parity checks and unknown horizon drops are silent in all three paths.
    98	**Impact**: consumers can receive divergent behavior without parity alarms.

   101	**Requirements**: REQ-003, REQ-005

   106	**Analysis**: both areas expose communication mismatches between declared resilience/freshness and actual behavior.
   107	**Impact**: operator decision confidence can be overstated.

     1	# Behavioral Requirements — ZINC-FUSION-V16
     2	> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.6 — Andrew Stellman
     3	> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16
     4	
     5	Version: v1.0
     6	Pipeline: contract-extraction v2 with narrative pass
     7	
     8	## Project Overview
     9	
    10	ZINC-FUSION-V16 is a commodity procurement forecasting platform focused on ZL futures price-level intelligence for buy-side operations. The system combines Supabase-hosted ingestion, Next.js API and UI surfaces, and a Python forecasting pipeline. Operational safety depends on contract alignment across SQL ingest writers, API envelopes, horizon normalization, and freshness semantics presented to procurement users.
    11	
    12	This requirements set is derived from Phase 1 exploration evidence in `quality/EXPLORATION.md` and targets the highest-risk divergence vectors discovered there: telemetry contract split, architecture/gate drift, fallback-contract mismatch, envelope inconsistency, mixed-vintage miscommunication, and duplicated horizon logic.
    13	
    14	## Use Cases
    15	
    16	### UC-01: Record an ingest run lifecycle event across SQL and TS writers
    17	
    18	- Actors: pg_cron SQL functions, API helper writer.
    19	- Preconditions: An ingest job starts, succeeds, or fails.
    20	- Steps:
    21	  1. Writer allocates or receives a run identifier.
    22	  2. Writer emits start record to `ops.ingest_run`.
    23	  3. Writer updates same run record to terminal status and timestamps.
    24	- Postconditions: Telemetry rows are query-consistent across writers.
    25	- Alternative paths: On ingest failure, terminal status and error message are still written.
    26	- Requirements: REQ-001
    27	
    28	### UC-02: Verify architecture-compliant auth and gate behavior without cron-route dependency
    29	
    30	- Actors: Middleware, verification scripts.
    31	- Preconditions: Protected route request or verification run.
    32	- Steps:
    33	  1. Middleware enforces auth/session rules.
    34	  2. Verification gates evaluate architecture compliance.
    35	  3. No component assumes `/api/cron` surface exists.
    36	- Postconditions: Compliant builds are not blocked by forbidden-route checks.
    37	- Alternative paths: Gate outputs actionable architecture mismatch evidence.
    38	- Requirements: REQ-002
    39	
    40	### UC-03: Serve intraday ZL bars with deterministic fallback semantics
    41	
    42	- Actors: `/api/zl/intraday` route.
    43	- Preconditions: User requests intraday bars.
    44	- Steps:
    45	  1. Route loads primary 15m dataset.
    46	  2. If primary unavailable, route follows explicitly documented fallback behavior.
    47	  3. Response contract communicates the data-source path used.
    48	- Postconditions: Client expectations match real behavior.
    49	- Alternative paths: If no fallback exists, route and docs declare no-fallback explicitly.
    50	- Requirements: REQ-003
    51	
    52	### UC-04: Enforce consistent envelope contract across forecast and dashboard APIs
    53	
    54	- Actors: API routes, contract types, parity gate scripts.
    55	- Preconditions: Success or failure responses emitted by covered endpoints.
    56	- Steps:
    57	  1. Contract type declares required and optional fields.
    58	  2. Route handlers serialize envelopes accordingly.
    59	  3. Gate checks validate only declared requirements.
    60	- Postconditions: Parity failures indicate product defects, not harness drift.
    61	- Alternative paths: Endpoint-specific exceptions are documented and consistently enforced.
    62	- Requirements: REQ-004
    63	
    64	### UC-05: Render risk-factor freshness with transparent mixed-vintage semantics
    65	
    66	- Actors: Risk-factor API and dashboard card UI.
    67	- Preconditions: Component timestamps differ across factors.
    68	- Steps:
    69	  1. API emits min/max/as-of and mixed-vintage fields.
    70	  2. UI shows degraded-state freshness messaging.
    71	  3. Operator can distinguish globally stale from partially stale vectors.
    72	- Postconditions: Procurement timing decisions use correct recency confidence.
    73	- Alternative paths: If metadata absent, UI displays explicit unknown-freshness state.
    74	- Requirements: REQ-005
    75	
    76	### UC-06.a: Normalize horizon values in `/api/zl/forecast`
    77	
    78	- Actors: Forecast route.
    79	- Preconditions: Rows include `horizon_days` and `model_version`.
    80	- Steps: Apply canonical allowlist and legacy remap.
    81	- Postconditions: Returned series uses canonical horizon set.
    82	- Requirements: REQ-006
    83	
    84	### UC-06.b: Normalize horizon values in `/api/zl/target-zones`
    85	
    86	- Actors: Target-zones route.
    87	- Preconditions: Rows include `horizon_days` and `model_version`.
    88	- Steps: Apply same normalization logic as UC-06.a.
    89	- Postconditions: Target-zone horizons align with forecast horizons.
    90	- Requirements: REQ-006
    91	
    92	### UC-06.c: Normalize horizon values in `/api/zl/forecast-targets`
    93	
    94	- Actors: Forecast-targets route.
    95	- Preconditions: Rows include `horizon_days` and `model_version`.
    96	- Steps: Apply same normalization logic as UC-06.a and UC-06.b.
    97	- Postconditions: Probability-surface horizons align with other forecast surfaces.
    98	- Requirements: REQ-006
    99	
   100	## Cross-Cutting Concerns
   101	
   102	- **Architecture authority:** Repository policy (`AGENTS.md`) is authoritative over historical middleware or gate assumptions.
   103	- **Telemetry integrity:** Ingest observability must stay coherent across language boundaries (SQL and TypeScript writers).
   104	- **Contract traceability:** API contract types, route payloads, and gate scripts must remain synchronized.
   105	- **Degradation transparency:** Fallback and mixed-vintage behaviors must be explicit in machine and user-facing surfaces.

   109	### Ingestion Observability and Lifecycle Contracts
   110	
   111	#### REQ-001: `ops.ingest_run` writers MUST use one normalized run contract
   112	
   113	- Functional section: Ingestion Observability and Lifecycle Contracts
   114	- Tier: 3
   115	- Pattern: parity
   116	- References: `supabase/migrations/202603180009_ops_vegas.sql:3-14`; `supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql:50-52`; `supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql:55-57`; `lib/server/ingest-run.ts:3-4`
   117	- Linked use cases: UC-01
   118	- Requirement: Every SQL and TypeScript writer that inserts or updates `ops.ingest_run` MUST include stable `run_id` lifecycle semantics and one canonical status vocabulary.
   119	- Conditions of satisfaction:
   120	  1. `ops.ingest_run` DDL defines `run_id UUID PRIMARY KEY` and writer inserts honor that key.
   121	  2. Each writer emits start and terminal state for the same `run_id`.
   122	  3. Status values are normalized (no mixed uppercase/lowercase contract split).
   123	  4. Error paths log terminal status with timestamp and error detail.
   124

   126

   130	- Tier: 3

   132	- References: `AGENTS.md:44-45`; `AGENTS.md:149-160`; `lib/supabase/proxy.ts:15-42`; `scripts/verify/gate3.sh:5`
   133	- Linked use cases: UC-02
   134	- Requirement: Middleware and verification logic MUST treat pg_cron-only architecture as authoritative and MUST NOT enforce `/api/cron` route presence.
   135	- Conditions of satisfaction:
   136	  1. Middleware rules do not carve out `/api/cron` behavior that contradicts architecture policy.
   137	  2. Gate scripts verify policy-conformant surfaces instead of forbidden route patterns.
   138	  3. Documentation and scripts share the same architecture truth source.
   139
